- Rule Id (if any, e.g. SC1000): 
- My shellcheck version (`shellcheck --version` or "online"): 
- [x] The rule's wiki page does not already cover this (e.g. https://shellcheck.net/wiki/SC2086)
- [x] I tried on https://www.shellcheck.net/ and verified that this is still a problem on the latest commit

#### For new checks and feature suggestions
- [x] https://www.shellcheck.net/ (i.e. the latest commit) currently gives no useful warnings about this

#### <img src="https://avatars.githubusercontent.com/u/2818758?u=40d36e49d938fda80abd46d6347b9bace1f73dd4&v=4" width="50">[koalaman](https://github.com/koalaman) commented at [2021-06-08 22:35](https://github.com/koalaman/shellcheck/issues/2236#issuecomment-857226621):

There is already a warning for this in version 0.7.2:

```
gzcat yesterday.log.gz | grep "$USER" < today.log
                                      ^-- SC2259: This redirection overrides piped input. To use both, merge or pass filenames.
```

If I misunderstood, please explain and reopen
